# ESG News Week In Review: 26 April – 03 May
[ESG](https://esgnews.com/category/esg/)
/
[ESG News Week In Review](https://esgnews.com/category/esg-news-week-in-review/)
/
[ESG Reporting](https://esgnews.com/category/esg-reporting/)

# ESG News Week In Review: 26 April – 03 May
by [ESG News Editorial Team](https://esgnews.com/author/esg-news-editorial-team/) • May 5, 2026
Share:
In this week’s ESG News Week In Review, energy security and geopolitical risk reshaped climate policy direction. China and India reduced fossil fuel reliance as renewables overtook coal, while global markets reacted to a $100 oil shock triggered by conflict, prompting governments to intervene and reassess energy strategies. At the same time, regulators advanced ESG infrastructure, with the FCA launching an ESG ratings pilot and global standards bodies moving closer to updated reporting frameworks.
For investors and operators, capital and execution continue to concentrate in scale. Octopus committed $500M to carbon removal, major forestry and reforestation funds expanded across Latin America and Africa, and advanced nuclear, battery storage, and renewables projects accelerated globally. The signal is clear: energy resilience, carbon integrity, and infrastructure scale are now defining competitive advantage.
#### **GOVERNMENT, POLICY & REGULATION**
  * [**China And India Cut Fossil Fuel Power As Renewables Overtake Coal In 2025**](https://esgnews.com/china-and-india-cut-fossil-fuel-power-as-renewables-overtake-coal-in-2025/)
  * [**Ireland Expands Energy Alliances With Spain, UK To Boost Interconnection And Security**](https://esgnews.com/ireland-expands-energy-alliances-with-spain-uk-to-boost-interconnection-and-security/)
  * [**FCA Launches ESG Ratings Pilot to Shape UK Reporting Rules Ahead of Regulation**](https://esgnews.com/fca-launches-esg-ratings-pilot-to-shape-uk-reporting-rules-ahead-of-regulation/)
  * [**EFRAG Calls For European Input As ISSB Advances SASB Standards Revisions**](https://esgnews.com/efrag-calls-for-european-input-as-issb-advances-sasb-standards-revisions/)
  * [**Middle East War Triggers $100 Oil Shock As Governments Cut Demand And Intervene In Energy Markets**](https://esgnews.com/middle-east-war-triggers-100-oil-shock-as-governments-cut-demand-and-intervene-in-energy-markets/)
  * [**US Ends Offshore Wind Leases As $885 Million Shifts To Fossil Fuel Investments**](https://esgnews.com/us-ends-offshore-wind-leases-as-885-million-shifts-to-fossil-fuel-investments/)


#### **CARBON**
  * [**Octopus Energy Commits $500 Million to US Carbon Removal, Targets 50 Million Tonnes of CO₂**](https://esgnews.com/octopus-energy-commits-500-million-to-us-carbon-removal-targets-50-million-tonnes-of-co%e2%82%82/)
  * [**IBM Launches Envizi Emissions API to Streamline Corporate Carbon Reporting**](https://esgnews.com/ibm-launches-envizi-emissions-api-to-streamline-corporate-carbon-reporting/)
  * [**Boeing Secures 20,000 Tonnes of High-Quality Carbon Removal to Tackle Aviation Emissions**](https://esgnews.com/boeing-secures-20000-tonnes-of-high-quality-carbon-removal-to-tackle-aviation-emissions/)
  * [**Aviva Investors Funds Colombia Forest Project Targeting Over 6 Million Tonnes of Carbon Removal**](https://esgnews.com/aviva-investors-funds-colombia-forest-project-targeting-over-6-million-tonnes-of-carbon-removal/)

  * [**Climate Bonds Expands Bioenergy Criteria To Include Electricity, Tighten Methane Standards**](https://esgnews.com/climate-bonds-expands-bioenergy-criteria-to-include-electricity-tighten-methane-standards/)
  * [**Corporate Decarbonization Holds Steady Despite Policy Shifts, PwC Report Finds**](https://esgnews.com/corporate-decarbonization-holds-steady-despite-policy-shifts-pwc-report-finds/)

# ESG News Week In Review: 26 April – 03 May

# ESG News Week In Review: 26 April – 03 May
# ESG News Week In Review: 26 April – 03 May
[ESG](https://esgnews.com/category/esg/)
/
[ESG News Week In Review](https://esgnews.com/category/esg-news-week-in-review/)

[ESG Reporting](https://esgnews.com/category/esg-reporting/)

# ESG News Week In Review: 26 April – 03 May
by [ESG News Editorial Team](https://esgnews.com/author/esg-news-editorial-team/) • May 5, 2026
Share:
In this week’s ESG News Week In Review, energy security and geopolitical risk reshaped climate policy direction. China and India reduced fossil fuel reliance as renewables overtook coal, while global markets reacted to a $100 oil shock triggered by conflict, prompting governments to intervene and reassess energy strategies. At the same time, regulators advanced ESG infrastructure, with the FCA launching an ESG ratings pilot and global standards bodies moving closer to updated reporting frameworks.
For investors and operators, capital and execution continue to concentrate in scale. Octopus committed $500M to carbon removal, major forestry and reforestation funds expanded across Latin America and Africa, and advanced nuclear, battery storage, and renewables projects accelerated globally. The signal is clear: energy resilience, carbon integrity, and infrastructure scale are now defining competitive advantage.
#### **GOVERNMENT, POLICY & REGULATION**
  * [**China And India Cut Fossil Fuel Power As Renewables Overtake Coal In 2025**](https://esgnews.com/china-and-india-cut-fossil-fuel-power-as-renewables-overtake-coal-in-2025/)
  * [**Ireland Expands Energy Alliances With Spain, UK To Boost Interconnection And Security**](https://esgnews.com/ireland-expands-energy-alliances-with-spain-uk-to-boost-interconnection-and-security/)
  * [**FCA Launches ESG Ratings Pilot to Shape UK Reporting Rules Ahead of Regulation**](https://esgnews.com/fca-launches-esg-ratings-pilot-to-shape-uk-reporting-rules-ahead-of-regulation/)
  * [**EFRAG Calls For European Input As ISSB Advances SASB Standards Revisions**](https://esgnews.com/efrag-calls-for-european-input-as-issb-advances-sasb-standards-revisions/)
  * [**Middle East War Triggers $100 Oil Shock As Governments Cut Demand And Intervene In Energy Markets**](https://esgnews.com/middle-east-war-triggers-100-oil-shock-as-governments-cut-demand-and-intervene-in-energy-markets/)
  * [**US Ends Offshore Wind Leases As $885 Million Shifts To Fossil Fuel Investments**](https://esgnews.com/us-ends-offshore-wind-leases-as-885-million-shifts-to-fossil-fuel-investments/)


#### **CARBON**
  * [**Octopus Energy Commits $500 Million to US Carbon Removal, Targets 50 Million Tonnes of CO₂**](https://esgnews.com/octopus-energy-commits-500-million-to-us-carbon-removal-targets-50-million-tonnes-of-co%e2%82%82/)
  * [**IBM Launches Envizi Emissions API to Streamline Corporate Carbon Reporting**](https://esgnews.com/ibm-launches-envizi-emissions-api-to-streamline-corporate-carbon-reporting/)
  * [**Boeing Secures 20,000 Tonnes of High-Quality Carbon Removal to Tackle Aviation Emissions**](https://esgnews.com/boeing-secures-20000-tonnes-of-high-quality-carbon-removal-to-tackle-aviation-emissions/)
  * [**Aviva Investors Funds Colombia Forest Project Targeting Over 6 Million Tonnes of Carbon Removal**](https://esgnews.com/aviva-investors-funds-colombia-forest-project-targeting-over-6-million-tonnes-of-carbon-removal/)
  * [**Isometric, Verde Move to Scale Carbon Removal Credits Through Infrastructure**](https://esgnews.com/isometric-verde-move-to-scale-carbon-removal-credits-through-infrastructure/)


#### **CLIMATE & ENERGY TRANSITION**
